   function loadZopim(path, caller) {
        window.$zopim || (function(d, s) {
            var z = window.$zopim = function(c) {
                z._.push(c);
            };

            var $ = z.s = d.createElement(s);
            var e = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
            z.set = function(o) {
                z.set._.push(o);
            };
            z._ = [];
            z.set._ = [];
            $.async = !0;
            $.setAttribute('charset', 'utf-8');
            $.src = '//v2.zopim.com/?2idAW3AKZ28UUWgitXg7WMvt1MrRI4pX';
            z.t = +new Date();
            $.type = 'text/javascript';
            e.parentNode.insertBefore($, e);
        })(document, 'script');

        $zopim(function() {
            if (sessionStorage.getItem('showZopimHomepage') == null) {
                sessionStorage.setItem('showZopimHomepage', Math.floor(Math.random() * 101) < 60);
            }

            if (path.includes(caller.stringLocalizer.localizedLink('/contactus')) ||
                path.includes(caller.stringLocalizer.localizedLink('/help')) ||
                path.startsWith(caller.stringLocalizer.localizedLink('/help/topic/')) ||
                (path == caller.stringLocalizer.localizedLink('/') && sessionStorage.getItem('showZopimHomepage') == "true")) {

                $zopim.livechat.theme.setColor('#4C394E');

                var first_time = true;
                $zopim.livechat.setOnStatus(function(status) {

                    if (!first_time) return;

                    first_time = false;
                    if (status == 'online') {
                        $zopim.livechat.button.show();
                    } else if ($zopim.livechat.isChatting() == "false") {
                        $zopim.livechat.button.hide();
                    }
                });

                $zopim.livechat.setOnChatStart(function() {
                    if ($zopim.livechat.isChatting() == "true") {
                        $zopim.livechat.window.show();
                        $zopim.livechat.bubble.show();
                    }
                });

                $zopim.livechat.window.onHide(function() {
                    $zopim.livechat.button.show();
                });

                $zopim.livechat.window.onShow(function() {
                    $zopim.livechat.window.show();
                });

                if ($zopim.livechat.window.getDisplay() == "true") {
                    $zopim.livechat.hideAll();
                }

            } else {
                $zopim.livechat.hideAll();
            }

        });
    }
